adjusted diluted EPS increased 7% to $2.49</font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%;padding-left:5.5pt">Maintaining fiscal 2026 consolidated outlook for revenue growth of 5% to 6%, adjusted EBIT margin expansion of 50 to 70 basis points, and adjusted diluted EPS growth of 8% to 10%</font></div><div style="text-indent:9pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:138%">ROSELAND, N.J. &#8211; October&#160;29, 2025</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%"> &#8211; ADP (Nasdaq&#58; ADP), a global leader in HR and payroll solutions, today announced its first quarter fiscal 2026 financial results and updated its fiscal 2026 outlook.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:138%">First Quarter Fiscal 2026 Consolidated Results</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">Compared to last year&#8217;s first quarter, revenues increased 7% to $5.2 billion and 6% on an organic constant currency basis. Net earnings increased 6% to $1.0 billion, and adjusted net earnings increased 6% to $1.0 billion. Adjusted EBIT increased 7% to $1.3 billion, and adjusted EBIT margin remained flat at 25.5%. ADP&#8217;s effective tax rate for the quarter was 22.5% on both a reported basis and an adjusted basis. Diluted EPS increased 6% to $2.49, and adjusted diluted EPS increased 7% to $2.49.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">&#8220;Fiscal 2026 started off with solid financial performance and meaningful progress across our strategic priorities,&#8221; said Maria Black, President and Chief Executive Officer, ADP. &#8220;We continue to drive strong outcomes for clients, as exemplified by our record client satisfaction levels and continued robust retention results. We also continue to infuse AI into our products and across our operations to solve real-world HR problems and fundamentally shift how work gets done.&#8221; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">&#8220;Our first quarter revenue and margin performance exceeded our expectations, as we benefited from solid new business bookings growth, strong client revenue retention, and higher client funds interest revenue,&#8221; said Peter Hadley, Chief Financial Officer, ADP. &#8220;We look forward to delivering strong financial performance in fiscal 2026, as we continue to make strategic investments to support our long-term growth.&#8221;</font></div><div style="height:42.75pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">1</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:42.75pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:138%">Adjusted EBIT, adjusted EBIT margin, adjusted net earnings, adjusted diluted earnings per share, adjusted effective tax rate and organic constant currency are all non-GAAP financial measures.
